It also maps your home and can be controlled using the app, Amazon Alexa, or Google Assistant.</p>\n\n<h3>Best robot vacuums for pet hair, ranked by Smarts and Conveniences</h3>\n\n<ol>\n<li>iRobot Roomba i7+</li>\n<li>Roborock S6 </li>\n<li>iRobot Roomba 980 </li>\n<li>Neato Botvac D6 </li>\n<li>Shark Ion R85 </li>\n</ol>\n\n<h3>Price (lowest to highest)</h3>\n\n<p>If you're simply looking for a frugal option to help you clean up after your beloved pets, then it helps to know which vacuums can suck up fur without costing too much. Just be aware that you typically pass up certain conveniences by choosing less expensive units.</p>\n\n<p>The iLife V3s Pro is the least expensive device that still works well in pet homes. It doesn't come with an app, but you'll still be able to control it using the included remote. Additionally, since it doesn't map your home, it will bounce around randomly, but it will do a good job cleaning the ground it covers. Just note that this device is specifically meant for hard floors and low-pile carpets.</p>\n\n<p>Despite being the second most inexpensive vacuum, you can start the Shark ION R85 using the included app. You can also set cleaning schedules or control the unit using Alexa or Google Assistant. This is a powerful device that can suck up fur and debris like dry pet food or cat litter. The tradeoff is that it doesn't map your home.</p>\n\n<p>Eufy's RoboVac 11S Max is a great little device for the money. </li>\n<li>The app has most of the features of the regular Dark Sky app with the exception of paid features. </li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>Dark Sky was a popular weather app that was <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/weather-app-dark-sky-will-disappear-android-after-apple-aquisition\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">purchased by Apple</a> earlier this year. As a result, it no longer works on Android as of August 1, with fans having to find replacements. Now, one <em>XDA</em> community developer has re-created the Dark Sky experience â€” literally.</p>\n\n<p>Dubbed Darker Sky, it's essentially the Dark Sky app itself back from the dead. It was built by reverse-engineering the Dark Sky APK and pairing with an iOS API key for the data.  Everything works but \"weather report submissions, weather notifications/alerts, and widgets.\"</p>\n\n<p>The folks over at <a href=\"https://www.xda-developers.com/dark-sky-android-bring-back/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><em>XDA Developers</em></a> provide some additional context, noting:</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n  <p>Darker Sky was made by a prolific developer and reverse engineer who wishes to remain anonymous since this modification was done on shaky grounds. It's a third-person platformer that sees players take on the role of either Ratchet â€” a Lombax who knows how to fight and repair â€” and Clank, his robotic sidekick.</p> \n   <p>It's unknown exactly how Rift Apart will follow the 2016 title, but from the looks of the trailer, rifts have begun popping up across the world, and it'll be up to Ratchet and Clank to get to the bottom of just what's causing the rifts and how to stop them.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"trailers\">Can I check out any Ratchet and Clank: Rift Apart <em>trailers</em>?</h2> \n   <div class=\"article-body__video\">\n    <div class=\"video_iframe\">\n     <iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/ai3o0XtrnM8?modestbranding=0&amp;html5=1&amp;rel=0&amp;autoplay=0&amp;wmode=opaque&amp;loop=0&amp;controls=1&amp;autohide=0&amp;showinfo=0&amp;theme=dark&amp;color=red&amp;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"682\" height=\"400\" class=\"video-filter video-youtube vf-ai3o0xtrnm8\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" loading=\"lazy\"></iframe>\n    </div>\n   </div> \n   <!--/video--> \n   <p>So far we've only received one trailer for Ratchet and Clank: Rift Apart, which is its reveal trailer from The Future of Gaming PS5 event. A VPN takes your Internet connection and makes it more secure, by cloaking your internet activity in anonymity and stops you from being tracked across the web for advertising, having your traffic intercepted, or running into malicious sites. They are also great if you want to access content that is blocked in your region as you can use one to appear as if you are in another country.</p> \n            <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/what-is-vpn\" title=\"\" class=\"cta norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">VPN 101: What is it?</a></p> \n            <p>You can run a VPN on everything from your computer or phone, to devices like your smart TV, Wi-Fi router, games console, and more. They come in at all different price points, so you're likely going to want to find a great VPN deal or discount to take advantage of when signing up.</p> \n            <h2 class=\"separator\">How do you pick the best VPN provider?</h2> \n            <p>There's so much to consider when deciding which VPN provider is right for you. Of course, you want to ensure it is available on all of the devices you wish to run it on, but you should also think about things like the service's server variety (both in number and physical location) to ensure you have a reliable connection and speed, what data (if any) may be logged, strength of the encryption used, ease-of-use, and the quality of customer support. On top of all of that, price may be a huge factor in your decision-making.</p> \n            <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/why-vpn-important-use\" title=\"\" class=\"cta norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">Why is it important to use a VPN?</a></p> \n            <p>As with many things in life, you tend to get what you pay for with VPNs. That being said, most providers will have a free trial or a money-back guarantee so you can try them out without risking your money. We've gathered up the best VPN deals above with the most pertinent information to help you make an informed choice.</p> \n            <h2 class=\"separator\">How to get the Best VPN Deals</h2> \n            <p>VPN providers generally offer better discounts the longer you subscribe for, so opting for a 3-year or 2-year plan is usually going to save you the most money. The majority of services have money-back guarantees so you can try out the apps on your devices and cancel your subscription if it's doesn't work out for you. Be sure to read the terms when signing up.</p> \n            <p>A few VPN services have free plans but these are usually restricted in terms of bandwidth. However, it can serve as a useful way to dip your toe into the VPN waters with no financial commitment. That being said, there are sometimes privacy implications with totally free services. If you're not paying for their product, they have to make their money back somewhere so make sure you take an in-depth look at the privacy policy for such services so you know what you're getting yourself in for.</p> \n            <p>We keep this list updated with the latest offers from the most reputable VPN providers, so bookmark it and check back in whenever you're in the market for a new VPN service. If you're unsure of which to choose, we have also put together <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/best-vpn\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">a comprehensive guide</a> on the best VPN services in 2020. We've also got a separate roundup highlighting the <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/best-free-vpn\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Best Free VPN Deals</a> that you might want to check out.</p> \n            <h2 class=\"separator\">Are there any free VPNs?</h2> \n            <p>The short answer here is yes. You can find some free VPN providers, but they may not be the best option for everyone. Often times you are trading off speed, reliability, data limits, and more to get a <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/best-free-vpn\" title=\"\" class=\"proj-anchor norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">free VPN</a>, which makes it ultimately more of a pain to actually use the service. With the costs mentioned above, you are better off spending a few bucks each month on your privacy instead of trying to make a free one work for you.</p> \n            <p>Some providers offer free trials, and some have money-back guarantees. If you aren't sure whether or not a VPN is right for you, this is a great way to test the waters.</p> \n            <h2 class=\"separator\">Can you use a VPN on your phone and PC?</h2> \n            <p>Most VPN providers allow you to have simultaneous connections, which means that you can connect up to a set amount of devices to the VPN service at the same time. Most companies offer up to five devices at once, though some are slightly lower or higher than that number. This allows you to keep it running on your phone, tablet, PC, and even streaming hardware without worrying about whether you need to disconnect another device to connect the new one or not. A neat way around this, if your provider of choice supports it, is running your VPN on your router so any device connected to your Wi-Fi network is automatically on the VPN while only using up 1 device slot!</p>\n           </hr>\n          </hr>\n         </hr>\n        </hr>\n       </hr>\n      </hr>\n     </hr>\n    </hr>\n   </hr>\n  </div>\n \n   <h2 id=\"overview\">What is Disney Plus?</h2> \n   <p>Disney+ is a streaming service that brings together all of the content in Disney's massive media empire â€” from Disney and Pixar to Marvel to Lucasfilm to National Geographic and 20th Century Fox â€” in one easy-to-use app. Available on nearly every single major platform and with hundreds of films and TV shows from the Disney Vault and recent theatrical releases, Disney+ is a tantalizing realization of a dream many Disney nerds (like myself) have had of being able to watch their favorite shows and films in one place rather than having to hunt for them across a half dozen services â€” and this is also the first time a great deal of legacy Disney television content is available for streaming.</p> \n   <p>In short, Disney+ is simply everything we ever wished it would be.</p> \n   <ul class=\"cta\"> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Disney+ review: A spell has been cast over my streaming heart</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <p>This is the future of video for Disney. Anything and everything that falls under the Disney umbrella â€” and make no mistake, it is a <em>huge</em> umbrella â€” will eventually go through the Disney+ app, on whatever platform you wish to watch it on. If that sounds impossibly big, well, you're right. But Disney has done well to pave this road with the also extremely successful ESPN+, which also is owned by Disney and runs on the same technology. (In fact, Disney bought the company that built the streaming side of ESPN+ in order to jumpstart Disney+'s development.)</p> \n   <p>The best part of Disney+ is that it is ridiculously easy to sign up for the service whether you're at your desktop computer or on the go with your phone.</p> \n   <ul class=\"cta\"> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-sign-disney-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">How to sign up for Disney+</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <h2 id=\"availability\">What countries is Disney Plus available in?</h2> \n   <ul class=\"col3\"> \n    <li>Australia</li> \n    <li>Austria</li> \n    <li>Canada</li> \n    <li>France</li> \n    <li>Germany</li> \n    <li>India</li> \n    <li>Ireland</li> \n    <li>Italy</li> \n    <li>Japan</li> \n    <li>Monaco</li> \n    <li>Netherlands</li> \n    <li>New Zealand </li> \n    <li>Spain</li> \n    <li>Switzerland</li> \n    <li>United Kingdom</li> \n    <li>United States</li> \n   </ul> \n   <p>The above countries have Disney+ right now and the next batch of countries getting it on <strong>September 15, 2020</strong> includes Belgium, Denmark, Finland, Iceland, Luxembourg, Norway, Portugal, and Sweden. Keep an eye here for more information as it's made available.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"platforms\">What <em>devices</em> support Disney Plus?</h2> \n   <p>Disney+ is available on <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/what-devices-can-you-watch-disney-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">quite a few devices</a> at launch, but it's not as universally available as Netflix â€” yet. Whether you're on a phone, laptop, TV or gaming console built in the last 3 years, chances are Disney+ is available right now or will be available soon.</p> \n   <h3>iPhone and Android devices</h3> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus\" title=\"Disney Plus: How to sign up, exclusive 2020 content guide, movies &amp; more\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2019/04/disney-plus-platform-screenshot-investor-day-1vc8-1vc8.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Disney+ is available on <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-plus-phone\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Android phones</a> <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-plus-tablet\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">and tablets</a>, as well as Apple <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-plus-iphone-and-ipad\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">iPhones and iPads</a>. The benefit of using Disney+ on a phone or tablet rather than watching on a smart TV is that on these devices you <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/does-disney-allow-you-watch-movies-offline\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">can download videos</a> for offline playback, which is something you can do on up to 10 devices per Disney+ account, meaning everyone on the plan can keep a few videos downloaded in case of emergencies like being trapped on a Wi-Fi-less flight.</p> \n   <h3>Desktop and laptop computers</h3> \n   <p>Like all modern streaming services, Disney+ allows you to stream directly from <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fdisneyplus.bn5x.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F705874%2F9358%3FsubId1%3DUUacUdUnU74016YYr%26subId2%3Ddac%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.disneyplus.com%252F&amp;token=glAx8Ozz\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">DisneyPlus.com</a> on <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-plus-desktop\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Windows, MacOS, and Chrome OS computers</a> (sorry, Linux). You can't download videos for offline playback when streaming through the browser, but you do have some handy keyboard controls.</p> \n   <p>If you're on a Chromebook, just keep in mind you'll probably have it <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-plus-chromebook\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">error out the first time you try to watch</a> but after a quick refresh it should work just fine. Chromebooks are also the only laptops that can download videos for offline playback because Chromebooks also use they can use the Android app via Google Play.</p> \n   <p>It's rather unfortunate that Disney didn't release a Universal Windows Platform (UWP) app, especially since in order to release an Xbox One app, they've already done most of the work needed to make one. Since 4K streaming isn't currently supported when streaming through the website, a UWP would be a great way to allow Windows 10 media PCs to stream Disney+ in UHD.</p> \n   <ul class=\"cta\"> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/disney-needs-release-its-app-windows10\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Why Disney needs to release its Disney+ Xbox app for Windows 10 PCs</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <h3>Xbox, PlayStation &amp; Streaming Hardware</h3> \n   <p>Most people want to stream on a bigger screen so that they can enjoy Disney+ with their friends and family, and that means that supporting the gaming and entertainment consoles that we use now more than ever. Support for <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus-android-tv\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Android TV</a>, <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-roku\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Roku devices</a>, <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-plus-chromecast\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Google Chromecast</a>, <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-apple-tv\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Apple TV</a> and <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-amazon-fire-tv\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Fire TV devices</a> has been here since launch day.</p> \n   <p>On the gaming console side, both the <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-playstation\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">PlayStation 4 series</a> and <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-xbox\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Xbox One series</a> are supported right now, and the upcoming PS5 and Xbox Series X are expected to be supported when they launch at the end of the year. I honestly believe that gaming consoles are the best for watching Disney+ because you can use your <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/one-feature-every-streaming-service-needs-steal-disney-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">controller triggers</a> to fast forward and rewind more easily than using the on-screen controls.</p> \n   <p>On the mobile console side of the equation, no mobile consoles are currently supported, although Disney has hinted at bringing Disney+ to <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-plus-nintendo-switch\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Nintendo Switch</a> in the future. We have no concrete timeline on when it could launch on Switch, though.</p> \n   <h3>Smart TVs</h3> \n   <p>Smart TVs is one area where Disney+ has somewhat limited support at the moment. Only a handful of Smart TVs have Disney+ apps at the moment:</p> \n   <ul> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/does-disney-plus-work-lg-tvs\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">LG TVs running Web OS 3.0 produced in or after 2016</a></li> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/does-disney-plus-work-samsung-tvs\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Samsung TVs running Tizen OS produced in or after 2016</a></li> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/does-disney-plus-work-sony-tvs\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Sony TVs running Android TV</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <p>Beyond these brands, there's support for TVs that run <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus-android-tv\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Android TV</a>, <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-amazon-fire-tv\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Amazon Fire TV</a>, or <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/can-you-watch-disney-roku\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Roku TV</a> through their respective app stores. This is great news because you can't stream Disney+ through browsers on Smart TVs. <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/does-disney-plus-work-vizio-tvs\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Vizio TVs</a> don't have a built-in app for Disney+, but can use Chromecast built-in and Apple AirPlay.</p> \n   <h3>Which devices support Disney+ in 4K?</h3> \n   <p>There's more UHD content on Disney+ right now than I thought there'd be, but unfortunately playing it will require a 4K Smart TV that supports UHD playback â€” or an 4K supported entertainment console connected to a 4K TV that supports HDCP 2.2 â€” so even if you have a 4K screen hooked up to your gaming PC, you won't be streaming 4K that way. There are <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/which-devices-does-disney-plus-support-4k\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">plenty of 4K devices supported</a>, such as the NVIDIA Shield TV 2019, as well as a whole host of <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/best-4k-tvs-disney-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">excellent 4K TVs</a> at every price point from $300 to $3000.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"catalog\">What shows and movies are on Disney Plus?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus\" title=\"Disney Plus: How to sign up, exclusive 2020 content guide, movies &amp; more\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2019/11/disney-plus-marvel-section-briefcase.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Disney has prided itself on its Vault of extensive content for decades. While the Disney Vault strategy was starting to decay in the digital age, Disney+ will reap most of its rewards by hosting most of the Disney Vault as well as an impressive array of content from Marvel, Lucasfilm, Fox, and National Geographic. Right now, Disney+ has about 500 films and over 7,500 TV episodes, including most of films in the Marvel Infinity Saga and Star Wars Skywalker Saga.</p> \n   <ul class=\"cta\"> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/what-movies-does-disney-plus-have\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Every movie available on Disney+ in the US</a></li> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/what-tv-shows-does-disney-plus-have\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Every TV series available on Disney+ in the US</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <p>There's tons to watch, but unfortunately Disney didn't see fit to put all of its films in ordered playlists for easy marathoning. This would be especially handy for the Marvel Cinematic Universe, but since Disney doesn't have a handy playlist, we went ahead and made one so you can focus on prepping snacks for your Marvel movie marathon!</p> \n   <ul class=\"cta\"> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus-marvel-mcu-marathon\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Watch the MCU in chronological order with our trusty list!</a></li> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-watch-all-star-wars-movies-right-order\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Watch the Star Wars movies in the best order</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <p>Speaking of tons to watch, I waited a long time to get all of my favorite shows and movies in one easy-to-use place, and as such that meant that I had a long list of things I needed to watch, rewatch, and rewatch again because it's been so long since I've seen them. These are <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/first-16-disney-titles-im-watching-day-one\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">the first 16 films and shows I watched on Disney+.</a></p> \n   <h3>What more can I watch with the Disney Plus Bundle?</h3> \n   <p>Disney+ is just one of the major digital platforms Disney is serving up in this new streaming era. It's the largest, for sure. But it's also just one part of the puzzle.</p> \n   <ul class=\"cta\"> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-sign-disney-plus-bundle-ad-free-hulu\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Want to keep your ad-free Hulu with the Disney+ bundle? Here's how</a></li> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-switch-disney-plus-disney-bundle-hulu-and-espn-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">How to upgrade from Disney+ to the Disney+ bundle with ESPN+ and Hulu</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <h3>Have a look at ESPN+</h3> \n   <p>If nothing else â€” and if you're a sports fan of any kind â€” you also should consider a subscription with ESPN+. It runs on the same underlying platform as Disney+, so you'll be pretty familiar with how things work.</p> \n   <p>And as for the content, well. If you thought there was a lot of sports of TV, wait until you get a look at ESPN+. Yes, it's got live sports. All kinds of live sports. It's got <a href=\"https://www.cordcutters.com/espn-plus-college-football\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">college football games that you can't find on TV</a>. It's got a <a href=\"https://www.cordcutters.com/espn-plus-nhl\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">smattering of NHL</a>. Think Peyton Manning was resting in his retirement? Not quite. <em>Peyton's Places</em> is keeping him plenty busy. Plus football coach <em>Les Miles</em> has a show, you can find the irreplaceable duo of Boomer and TJ â€” and so much more, right there on ESPN+.</p> \n   <p>And, yes, you can <a href=\"https://www.cordcutters.com/how-watch-espn-your-tv\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">watch ESPN+ on your TV</a>, too.</p> \n   <h3 class=\"category reco-block\">More sports!</h3> \n   <h4 class=\"product\">ESPN+</h4> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus\" title=\"Disney Plus: How to sign up, exclusive 2020 content guide, movies &amp; more\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2019/11/espn-plus-logo-newer.png\" /></a></p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fgo.web.plus.espn.com%2Fc%2F221109%2F555830%2F9070%3FsubId1%3DUUacUdUnU74016YYr%26subId2%3Ddac%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fplus.espn.com%252F&amp;token=O_xqgzET\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$5/month at ESPN+</a></p> \n   <p class=\"subtitle\">Watch it all</p> \n   <p class=\"end\">ESPN+ is the perfect companion to Disney+ if you're a sports fan. There simply is no limit to the off-TV games you'll be able to watch, plus tons of original content.</p> \n   <h3>And don't forget Hulu</h3> \n   <p>The third arm of the trifecta is Hulu, which also is controlled by Disney. It's where you'll find all the on-demand content you've come to know from that service, as well as original shows like <em>The Handmaid's Tale</em>. Hulu is where much content originally planned for Disney+ is ending up as Disney tries to keep Disney+ to more family-friendly fare, so the bundle will de the only way to ensure that you can see <strong>all</strong> of the content that's coming down the pipeline.</p> \n   <p>And perhaps more important for Disney's purposes is Hulu with Live TV which, as the name implies, gets you <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Ftrack.flexlinkspro.com%2Fa.ashx%3Ffoid%3D1146973.142192125%26foc%3D2%26fot%3D9999%26fos%3D1&amp;token=bqA8H8g5\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">live (and local) television</a> alongside all that other content. You can now get the Disney+ bundle with Hulu + Live TV, which allows you to watch current Disney Channel shows â€” and tons more channels â€” along with legacy shows and older seasons on Disney+.</p> \n   <h2 class=\"category reco-block\">Stream this</h2> \n   <h3 class=\"product\">Hulu</h3> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus\" title=\"Disney Plus: How to sign up, exclusive 2020 content guide, movies &amp; more\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2018/09/hulu-logo-392.png\" /></a></p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Ftrack.flexlinkspro.com%2Fa.ashx%3Ffoid%3D1146973.140875248%26foc%3D1%26fot%3D9999%26fos%3D1&amp;token=4DL0fBzH\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">From $6/month at Hulu</a></p> \n   <p class=\"subtitle\">The full Hulu experience is expansive</p> \n   <p class=\"end\">Hulu becomes even more appealing when it gets bundled with Disney+ and ESPN+ for just $12.99 a month. Still to come is how much extra Live TV might cost under that plan.</p> \n   <h3>How does the Disney Plus library compare outside the US?</h3> \n   <p>There are differences in available content between countries â€” for instance, French law forbids theatrically released films from being put on a streaming service in that country for three years, so don't expect to see <em>Avengers: Endgame</em> on Disney+ in France until 2021 unless Disney manages some true shenanigans or gets that law changed somehow.</p> \n   <p>So far, however, the differences between the available content in the United States, Canada, and the Netherlands has been small, mainly that a few more of the recent Marvel and Disney films are currently unavailable.</p> \n   <ul class=\"cta\"> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/what-disney-plus-content-missing-canada\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">What Disney+ content is missing in Canada?</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <h3>How long will it take for new movies to be added to Disney Plus?</h3> \n   <p>The newest films in Disney's repertoire aren't available on Disney+ right now, but for most of them we won't be waiting too long. Movies will launch on Disney+ after the full theatrical and home video release, which will vary between individual films but should be 5-8 months after the theatrical release.</p> \n   <p>It's worth noting this general timeline has shifted a bit in 2020, as Onward, Frozen II and Hamilton all came to Disney+ significantly earlier than expected.</p> \n   <ul class=\"cta\"> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-long-will-it-take-movies-arrive-disney-plus-after-blu-ray-release\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">How long you'll have to wait for new movies to reach Disney+</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <h2 id=\"premier\">What is Disney+ Premier Access?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus\" title=\"Disney Plus: How to sign up, exclusive 2020 content guide, movies &amp; more\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2020/08/mulan-premier-access-china-pavilion.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>As the pandemic continues to keep theaters closed and push back big blockbuster releases, Disney has decided to do something new on Disney+ with the live-action remake: releasing it through Premier Access of Disney+. While the movie is still slated to release in theaters where Disney+ isn't available yet, in Disney+ markets, Disney will allow subscribers to unlock the movie early through Premier Access.</p> \n   <p>Premier Access is an upcharge feature inside Disney+: you buy the movie for $30 and unlock it for however long you continue to subscribe to Disney+. You can download the movie for offline playback on Android, iOS, and Chromebooks (through the Android app) and you can watch the movie as many times as you want, a significant change from other \"home premiere\" movies, which have been 48-hour rentals through one of the major digital retailers.</p> \n   <p>Films offered through Premier Access will eventually be available to all Disney+ subscribers, so if you don't want to pony up to watch it early, you'll probably be waiting 3-6 months to watch it through the main Disney+ catalog.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"features\">Parental controls, profiles, and account limits</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus\" title=\"Disney Plus: How to sign up, exclusive 2020 content guide, movies &amp; more\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2019/11/disney-plus-princess-collection-pixel-4.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Since Disney+ allows up to <strong>7 user profiles</strong> on a single account â€” and up to <strong>four users streams</strong> at a time â€” it's only natural that Disney+ accounts are meant to be shared amongst family. However, when the kids are misbehaving or when a friend isn't chipping in the way they promised they would when you let them have your login, it's time to <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-change-your-disney-plus-password\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">change the password</a> and lock them out!</p> \n   <p>It's very easy to get sucked in while watching your favorite shows on Disney+ â€” I put on an episode of Kim Possible to watch during lunch and then POW, it's dinnertime! â€” but if you want to give yourself a leg up against being sucked in by the siren song of the binge watch, <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-disable-autoplay-and-background-video-disney-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">turn off Autoplay</a>. Having to hit play every 20 or 40 minutes can help you break the cycle and get back to work, and since Autoplay is profile-based, you can turn it off for your kids account while leaving it on for yours.</p> \n   <p>As a streaming service that is geared so much towards towards families and kids, <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/does-disney-plus-have-parental-settings\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">parental controls on Disney+</a> are pretty simplistic at the moment: you can <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-create-childs-profile-disney-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">set up a child's profile</a> and set it to only allow content with a certain rating. Rather than giving age-based restrictions, Disney's content filter works based on the MPAA and US television content ratings systems, meaning that you'll have to decide if you want your child to see only G/TV-G content or allow in TV-Y7 and TV-Y7/FV.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"tipstricks\">How to get the most out of Disney Plus: Tips, tricks &amp; more</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus\" title=\"Disney Plus: How to sign up, exclusive 2020 content guide, movies &amp; more\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2019/11/disney-plus-app-settings-contrast.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Like any new, popular online service, Disney+ is not all smooth sailing, as magical as it may seem at first glance. Disney+ saw more users sign up on Day One as it expected in all of Year One, so overloaded servers have been the most prevalent problem so far, as evidenced by how widespread <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/error-83-disney-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Error 83</a> has been.</p> \n   <ul class=\"cta\"> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-fix-connection-issues-disney\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">How to fix connection issues with Disney+</a></li> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-fix-playback-issues-disney-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Having playback issues? Troubleshoot them here!</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <p>Of course, not all connection issues are related to server strain, you might need to check and make sure your <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/what-internet-speed-do-you-need-disney-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">internet is fast enough</a>. On some iPhones, you can get around Error 83 by switching from Wi-Fi to LTE, but you'll want to remember that streaming Disney+ that way can eat a capped <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-much-data-does-disney-plus-use\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">data plan</a> alive. When servers are slow or your network is down completely, you can still watch the Disney+ videos you downloaded to your phone, tablet, or Chromebook, at least.</p> \n   <ul class=\"cta\"> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-download-videos-disney-android\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">How to download videos on Disney+ for Android</a></li> \n    <li><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-download-videos-disney-plus-ios\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">How to download videos on Disney+ for iOS</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <h2 id=\"pricing\">How much does Disney Plus cost: Bundles, deals &amp; news-summary\">What you need to know</h2>\n\n<ul class=\"end\">\n<li>New U.S  restrictions on Huawei prevent the company from buying chips from U.S. linked companies, whether done through third-party intermediary.</p>\n\n<p>On Monday, <a href=\"https://www.reuters.com/article/us-usa-huawei-tech-idUSKCN25D1CC\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><em>Reuters</em></a> broke the news, reporting:</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n  <p>Commerce Secretary Wilbur Ross told Fox Business the restrictions on Huawei-designed chips imposed in May \"led them to do some evasive measures. They were going through third parties,\" Ross said. \"The new rule makes it clear that any use of American software or American fabrication equipment is banned and requires a license.\"</p>\n  \n  <p>Secretary of State Mike Pompeo said the rule change \"will prevent Huawei from circumventing U.S. law through alternative chip production and provision of off-the-shelf chips.\" He added in a statement \"Huawei has continuously tried to evade\" U.S. restrictions imposed in May.\n  The new actions, effective immediately, should prevent Huawei's attempts to circumvent U.S. export controls, Commerce said.</p>\n  \n  <p>It \"makes clear that we're covering off-the-shelf designs that Huawei may be seeking to purchase from a third-party design house,\" one Commerce Department official told Reuters.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p>Earlier this year, Huawei had <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/huawei-says-it-can-withstand-further-us-escalation\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">argued that it would be able to weather a storm</a> from the U.S. with little impact. Speaking at Davos, founder Ren Zhengfei said:</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n  <p>This year the U.S. might further escalate their campaign against Huawei, but I feel the impact on Huawei's business would not be very significant. experience.</li>\n<li>The proposed law will require tech giants such as Google and Facebook to pay media outlets for news and inform them in advance of any major algorithm changes that could affect their rankings. </li>\n<li>Google says the law will encourage large media companies to make \"enormous and unreasonable\" demands that could potentially put its free services at risk.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>Google Australia today published an <a href=\"https://about.google/intl/ALL_au/google-in-australia/an-open-letter/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">open letter</a> about the proposed News Media Bargaining Code on its homepage, telling users that the law could \"force\" it to provide them with a \"dramatically worse Google Search and YouTube.\"</p>\n\n<p>The open letter claims the proposed law will require Google to provide an unfair advantage to news media businesses over everyone else. Large news media businesses will be able to use the information from Google to improve their search rankings over competitors, even if someone else provides a better result. Google says search data of its Australian users may also be at risk, as the law will force the search giant to tell news media businesses \"how they can gain access\" to its users' data.</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n  <p>You've always relied on Google Search and YouTube to show you what's most relevant and helpful to you. We could no longer guarantee that under this law. The law would force us to give an unfair advantage to one group of businesses - news media businesses - over everyone else who has a website, YouTube channel or small business. News media businesses alone would be given information that would help them artificially inflate their ranking over everyone else, even when someone else provides a better result. We've always treated all website owners fairly when it comes to information we share about ranking. The proposed changes are not fair and they mean that Google Search results and YouTube will be worse for you.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p>Responding to Google's open letter, the Australian Competition and Consumer Commission (ACCC) released a <a href=\"https://www.accc.gov.au/media-release/response-to-google-open-letter\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">statement</a> saying the letter contains misinformation about the draft News Media Bargaining Code.</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n  <p>Google will not be required to charge Australians for the use of its free services such as Google Search and YouTube, unless it chooses to do so.</p>\n  \n  <p>Google will not be required to share any additional user data with Australian news businesses unless it chooses to do so.</p>\n  \n  <p>The draft code will allow Australian news businesses to negotiate for fair payment for their journalists' work that is included on Google services.</p>\n  \n  <p>This will address a significant bargaining power imbalance between Australian news media businesses and Google and Facebook.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p>As part of its news licensing program, which was <a href=\"https://www.blog.google/outreach-initiatives/google-news-initiative/licensing-program-support-news-industry-/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">announced</a> in June, Google had planned to team up with news publishers in Germany, Australia, and Brazil and pay them for their content. With content from Disney, Pixar, Fox, National Geographic, and Lucasfilm, Disney+ has been getting a lot of praise. Reviews <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/disney-plus-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">have been positive</a> and there are a lot of reasons to sign up for the service. Especially with a Verizon unlimited plan.</p> \n   <p>You can watch on more than your phone as well. With support for most major platforms, you can watch Disney+ on your TV, computer, tablet, and current generation game consoles. Quality is up to 4K with HDR with a compatible device. Video quality looks great on a smartphone display, especially OLED displays.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"wireless\">Which wireless plans include Disney Plus?</h2> \n   <p>For the original Disney+ on Us, all current and new Verizon Unlimited plans were eligible for a free year of Disney+. Now with Verizon and Disney's new agreement, the plans that get Disney + or the Disney Bundle are limited to the Play More Unlimited and Get More Unlimited plans, though the Start Unlimited and Do More Unlimited plans are eligible for six months of Disney+ for free.</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/free-disney-plus-verizon-what-you-need-know\" title=\"Free Disney Plus on Verizon: All the Details and How-to\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/08/verizon-disney-plans-breakdown.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>If you have an eligible account, all you need to do is <a href=\"https://login.verizonwireless.com/vzauth/UI/Login?realm=vzw&amp;goto=https%3A%2F%2Fmyvpostpay.verizonwireless.com%3A443%2Fmyv%2Fproductsapps%2F\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">add your Disney+ account to your Verizon account</a> in order to get that Disney movie magic back in your life. If you don't need hotspot capabilities, cloud storage, or free music streaming with Apple Music, this plan can be a good fit. Keep in mind that video only streams at 480p on this plan. This is a pretty barebones unlimited plan and doesn't come with any premium data, and it only comes with a 6-month trial of Disney+.</p> \n   <p>Premium data is what Verizon calls data that isn't deprioritized. This means that your data speeds will remain high even when a tower is crowded. Deprioritized data will have to wait in line a bit longer for its connection if the tower is at or above capacity. For most people, this won't be a huge issue and often will be unnoticeable, but for someone living in a dense area with congested networks, stepping up to the next plan can help your connection's  <blockquote class=\"pull\"> \n    <p>If you want to have Disney+ included beyond six months, your two choices are the $45/month Play More Unlimited or the $55/month Get More Unlimited.</p> \n   </blockquote> \n   <p>Like the base plan, Do More Unlimited only streams video at 480p but comes with a massive 50GB of premium data, you're free to stream much longer before you'll get slowed down. You get 15GB of LTE hotspot data so you can watch on some of your other devices if you're on the road. This plan only comes with a 6-month trial of Disney+.</p> \n   <p>If you want the highest quality video on the go, you'll need to grab the Play More Unlimited or Get More Unlimited plan. Both plans come with 720p video streaming and have Apple Music included. Play More Unlimited has 25GB of premium data with 15GB of LTE hotspot data. Get More Unlimited knocks it up another notch with 75GB of premium data and a 30GB LTE hotspot.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"datausage\">How much data does Disney Plus use?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/free-disney-plus-verizon-what-you-need-know\" title=\"Free Disney Plus on Verizon: All the Details and How-to\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2019/11/disney-plus-screenshot-download-quality.jpg?itok=PlU3V0xz\" /></a><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/free-disney-plus-verizon-what-you-need-know\" title=\"Free Disney Plus on Verizon: All the Details and How-to\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2019/11/disney-plus-screenshot-streaming-quality.jpg?itok=UR4UY5t8\" /></a></p> \n   <h3>Downloads</h3> \n   <p>The most consistent way to know how much data Disney+ will use in the app is to use the download feature. This saves the video file to your phone's storage so you can play it back without using your data connection. This can be a great way to save data by taking advantage of Wi-Fi and can be a lifesaver on long flights. It's also a good option for someone without premium data that wants a consistent video experience.</p> \n   <p>Downloads come in three flavors: standard, medium, and high. High actually uses significantly more data than standard or even medium. A 39 minute episode of The Mandalorian came in at 270Mb, 424MB, and 1.5GB across the three quality settings. Something shorter like the three minute Pixar short Forky Asks a Question: What is Money, comes in at 20MB, 31MB, 112MB. Both videos come in around 7MB, 10MB, and 38MB per minute of video.</p> \n   <div class=\"media-gallery-wrap\">\n    <div class=\"media-gallery\"> \n     <a <!--/media-gallery-->\n   </div> \n   <h3>Streaming</h3> \n   <p>Streaming video is always going to be less predictable and consistent that downloading. Streaming over cellular data comes in with the settings automatic and save data. On a strong LTE connection around 50Mbps down and set to automatic, I used about as much data as I would have downloading the video on high. Set to save data, I used closer to the medium setting. Both of these settings will drop the quality to avoid pauses if your connection quality is lower than it needs to be for the higher qualities.</p> \n   <p>For now, it's safe to assume you'll be operating around medium to high settings on streaming. To be honest, I couldn't see much of a difference on the smaller OLED screen on my phone.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"home\">Fios and 5G Home internet plans</h2> \n   <p>New customers on Verizon's home internet plans also got one year of Disney+ for free. Unlike the wireless plans, this only applied to new customers. There is no mention of a continued Disney+ bundle for FiOS at this time, but these plans may be expanded in the future.</p> \n   <table class=\"spec-table\"> \n    <thead> \n     <tr> \n does it cost?</h3> \n   <p>Disney+ costs $6.99 per month, or $69.99 per year in the United States normally. Your one-year subscription will pause until the Verizon promotion is over. You won't lose the service you paid for.</p> \n   <h3>How many devices can stream at once?</h3> \n   <p>Disney+ can be used on 10 unique devices but only four can stream at once. Still this is good for a family and might be one of the best things to happen to the family road trip since the Game Boy.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"signup\">How do I sign up?</h2> \n   <p>You will need to create a Disney+ account separately on <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fdisneyplus.bn5x.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F705874%2F9358%3FsubId1%3DUUacUdUnU82324YYr%26subId2%3Ddac%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.disneyplus.com%252F&amp;token=xouj5bO9\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Disney+</a>. field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p class=\"intro\">Panos Panay brings his hardware and software experience to Sonos' board.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/microsofts-panos-panay-joins-sonos-board-directors\" title=\"Microsoft's Panos Panay joins Sonos board of directors\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/sites/wpcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_blw/public/field/image/2019/10/panos-surface-laptop-3-open.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<h2 class=\"aside news-summary\">What you need to know</h2>\n\n<ul class=\"end\">\n<li>Panos Panay has been appointed to the board of directors of Sonos.</li>\n<li>Panay is in charge of the Windows + Devices team at Microsoft.</li>\n<li>Sonos values Panay's experience with hardware and software, including his several years at Microsoft.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>Sonos announced today that Panos Panay has been appointed to its board of directors (<a href=\"https://www.businesswire.com/news/home/20200817005117/en/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">via Business Wire</a>). Panay is most well-known for his work at Microsoft leading the hardware division, including Microsoft's innovative and successful <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/surface-duo\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Surface lineup</a>.</p>\n\n<p>Recently, <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/panos-panay-will-lead-windows-experience-addition-microsofts-hardware-efforts\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Panay's role at Microsoft expanded</a> to include both devices Windows. Panay's experience with both hardware and software is an asset valued by Sonos.</p>\n\n<p>\"Panos brings extensive experience in building powerful and engaging consumer hardware products and experiences that customers love, at a global scale. He understands how hardware and software work together to deliver products that are easy to use, and deliver a fantastic experience. His track record, along with his passion for Sonos, will make him an impactful contributor to the company's ongoing success.\" said Mike Volpi, Sonos chairman of the board.</p>\n\n<p>While a significant role, it's important to note that people can, and often do sit on the board of directors of companies while having full-time jobs elsewhere. This is going to be Walmart's answer to <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/tryprimefree?tag=androidcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUacUdUnU91420YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Amazon Prime</a>, a service with so many perks there has been little to compete against it for so long. Walmart does still have a few advantages over Amazon, though, and plans to push those leads through this new program. In particular, Walmart+ is going match Prime with free two-day shipping and add same-day grocery delivery on top of that. There will be a lot of other perks as well.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/walmart-plus\" title=\"Walmart Plus: Launch date, pricing information &amp; more\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2017/11/walmart-store-1.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/walmart-launching-amazon-prime-competitor-later-month\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Rumors had Walmart+ originally launching in the spring</a>, but the spread of COVID-19 led to a delay. Of course, everyone staying at home and shopping at home led to a spike in Walmart's sales, so it makes sense the company would want to capitalize off that momentum. Plus, Amazon has struggled to meet demand in a similar shopping spike thanks to the pandemic, so Walmart could definitely slip in and gain some ground there.</p>\n\n<p>As Walmart plans to roll out this exciting new service, we're going to be on top of all the newest information. We've got it all right here, and we'll continue to update this page as we find out more.</p>\n\n<h2>What is Walmart+?</h2>\n\n<p>Simply put, Walmart+ is Walmart's new upcoming membership. You pay an annual fee, you get perks. If you do most of your shopping at Walmart, or you used to and would like to go back to doing so, then Walmart+ is going to be of interest to you. Similar to Amazon Prime or a Costco membership, Walmart+ is going to give you some amazing perks just for using Walmart the way you always do.</p>\n\n<p>While it will cost you something, the benefits you get will pay for themselves. For example, if you order online at Walmart you know there is a shipping fee unless you order at least $35 worth of stuff. Amazon has a similar fee but Amazon Prime members don't have to worry about it. If you can get around that shipping cost, you're saving that money every time you order from Walmart. (It is unclear still if that threshold will go away for Walmart+ members, but it would make sense.)</p>\n\n<h2>When does Walmart+ launch?</h2>\n\n<p>As of right now, August 17, there is no clear indication of when the service is going to launch. There is a <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fgoto.walmart.com%2Fc%2F1943169%2F612734%2F9383%3Fsharedid%3D159229%26subId1%3DUUacUdUnU91420YYr%26subId2%3Ddac%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.walmart.com%252Fplus&amp;token=ppNFsgSx\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">website for it</a>, but all that says is \"Coming Soon.\" The rumor was that it was supposed to launch sometime in July after being delayed from its original launch in March or April. Unfortunately July passed with no clear indication of that happening. And now it looks like more of the same for August. Keep an eye out on this page and at Walmart for more information.</p>\n\n<h2>How much will Walmart+ cost?</h2>\n\n<p>That's the big question right? Similar to Amazon Prime, Walmart+ will be a subscription service requiring an annual payment. It looks like it will cost $98 a year, but it will also come with a lot of perks to justify that price. At this time it is still unknown whether Walmart will allow customers to pay for the service on a monthly basis, or if you will need to prepay for the whole year in order to sign up.</p>\n\n<h2>How does Walmart+ pricing compare to Amazon Prime?</h2>\n\n<p>Amazon Prime is currently $119, which means that Walmart+ comes in at $21 less. Prime does have a lot of ways to lower that price, though. Students can get many Prime benefits for half the cost. People on government assistance can get a discount. And you can always pay for it monthly instead of yearly if you don't need it the entire time. It's still unclear how many benefits like that will be offered by Walmart+ (if any).</p>\n\n<h2>What are the perks of Walmart+?</h2>\n\n<p>The three biggest perks include free two-day shipping when you order from Walmart, unlimited same-day grocery delivery from Walmart Supercenters, and a discount on fuel when using Walmart gas stations. Other perks will include early access to deals, reserved delivery slots, and access to Walmart Express, a new two-hour delivery offering similar to Amazon's Prime Now. It looks like Walmart might also bring back for Walmart+ members its Scan &amp; Go service that was discontinued a couple years back. This service allows you to check out in a Walmart store without waiting in line.</p>\n\n<p>Other potential perks that are probably still a ways off from actually happening include a Walmart+ credit card and a Walmart+ entertainment service. The latter would be a rival to Amazon Prime, the streaming service offered to Prime members, but Walmart is a long ways from bringing that to life. In the meantime, keep an eye on Camp by Walmart, which is a free service to any Walmart customer with the Walmart app. It is Walmart's first foray into digital entertainment and probably the precursor of bigger things to come.</p>\n\n<h2>What else should I know?</h2>\n\n<p>Walmart wants this to be a success. Amazon Prime has been around for 15 years at this point, and Amazon's online shopping has managed to surpass and dwarf Walmart in that time, despite Walmart being the next largest retailer in the U.S. It's a safe bet that they will continue to add more and more benefits over time to match whatever Amazon is doing.</p>\n\n<p>It also might not be perfect right out of the gate. It's not like people haven't tried to compete with Amazon Prime before. It's just very difficult. Espect a few hiccups along the way, but remember that Walmart has an amazing network of brick and mortar stores that can support this new endeavor in a way Amazon cannot.</p>\n\n<h2>Let Thrifter help you</h2>\n\n<p>Remember one of the key elements to this new Walmart+ benefit will be early access to deals, and with the guaranteed faster shipping times you'll be able to take advantage of all the discounts Walmart has.
